<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">State the aggregate market value&nbsp; of the voting and non-voting common equity held by non-affiliates computed by reference to the price at which the common equity was last sold, or the average bid and asked price of such common equity, as of the last business day of the registrants&#8217; most recently completed second fiscal quarter.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">The aggregate market value held by non-affiliates cannot be determined as the issuer&#8217;s common equity is currently not publicly traded.&nbsp; </FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">State the number of shares outstanding of each of the issuer's classes of common equity, as of the latest practicable date: The Registrant had 33,001,000 shares of common stock outstanding as of October 11, 2012.&nbsp; </FONT></P>

<h2 style="margin-bottom:3.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><a name="_Toc254620942"></a></h2>
<a name="_bclFooter4"></a><DIV>





<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 style="margin-bottom:3.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:normal;">ITEM 1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; DESCRIPTION OF
BUSINESS</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">History</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
were incorporated in the State of Nevada on March 11, 2011. Since inception, we
have been engaged in organizational efforts and obtaining initial financing.&#160;
We were initially formed as a vehicle to pursue a business combination. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;layout-grid-mode:line;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;layout-grid-mode:line;">We have not been involved in any bankruptcy,
receivership or similar proceeding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
February 8, 2012 we entered into a Licensing Agreement (the &#8220;Agreement&#8221;) with
Quadra International Inc. (&#8220;Quadra&#8221;), a manufacturer of the QI System.&#160; The QI
System processes organic waste into marketable by-products and is proprietary
technology.&#160; We obtained exclusive licensing rights in the states of Johore and
Selangor, Malaysia for a period of 25 years.&#160; We will have exclusive rights to
sub-license, establish joint ventures to commercialize, use and process organic
waste, and sell related by-products.&#160;&#160; The license fee is $ 40,000.&#160; We are
entitled to purchase the QI System at a fixed price of $ 400,000 for the term
of our license.&#160; We are subject to a royalty of 5% on licensee fees received
from appointed sub-licensees as well as 3% on gross sales from by-product
generated from any operated QI System in Johore and Selangor.&#160; We also have the
option of obtaining exclusive license rights in other states and federal
territories in Malaysia with license fees varying with each state and
territory.&#160; The Agreement was an arms-length transaction. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The&#160;
QI System is designed to handle commonly generated waste stream, whether
liquid, solid, mixed or unmixed (including whole tires, all types of plastics,
e-waste, shredder residues, sewage sludge, animal wastes, biomass, ligneous and
infectious biohazard medical waste) and represent an environmentally friendly
and commercially viable alternative to traditional methods of processing waste.
</font><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The </font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">solutions are commercially viable
ecological recycling models based on zero-waste philosophy. We will initially
be focused on using the application for processing waste tires for conversion
to biochar and fuel oil. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Current Business</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;layout-grid-mode:line;">Our business objective is to </font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">license the QI System through qualified interests and
establishing waste conversion operations through joint ventures.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
February 15, 2012, we entered into a Sub-License Agreement with Zhunger Capital
Partners Inc. (&#8220;Zhunger&#8221;), to grant exclusive rights to sub-license, establish
joint ventures to commercialize, use and process organic waste, and sell
related by-products for a period of 25 years in the state of Johore, Malaysia.
Zhunger will be subject to a sub-license fee of $ 70,000 payable in monthly installments
of $ 5,000 per month commencing March 1, 2012 ending, April 1, 2013.&#160; As per
our Agreement with Quadra, 5% of any sub license fees received is payable to
Quadra on a quarterly basis.&#160; As additional consideration, gross sales on
by-products generated from the QI System will be subject to a 5% royalty fee of
which 3% will be remitted to Quadra and 2% retained by us.&#160; Zhunger is entitled
to purchase the QI System (one treatment application &#8211; used tires) for a fixed
price of $ 400,000 for a period of 25 years. The agreement with Zhunger was an
arms-length transaction. We have entered into discussions to establish waste
conversion operations with Zhunger through a joint venture however an agreement
has not materialized. There can be no assurance that any agreements will
materialize. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Principal Products, Services and Their Markets</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
QI System has the capability of four applications for treatment of waste tires,
plastics, solid waste and hospital waste. The QI System we are entitled to
purchase at a price of $ 400,000 from Quadra will have one treatment
application for waste tires.&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<a name="_bclFooter5"></a><DIV>





<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
</DIV><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size=2><DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always">&nbsp;</div><a name="page_6"></a><a name="_bclPageBorder6"></a><DIV STYLE="WIDTH: 100%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%; PADDING-LEFT: 0%">

<a name="_bclHeader6"></a><DIV>





<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">How the System Works</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pyrolysis technologies: </font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pyrolysis
is most commonly used for organic materials. It does not involve reactions with
oxygen or any other reagents but can take place in their presence. Extreme
pyrolysis, which leaves only carbon as the residue, is called carbonization and
is also related to the chemical process of charring.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pyrolysis
is heavily used in the chemical industry, for example, to produce charcoal,
activated carbon, methyl alcohol and other chemicals from wood to convert
ethylene dichloride into vinyl chloride to make PVC, to produce coke fuel from
coal, to convert biomass into synthetic gas, to turn waste into safely
disposable substances, and for the cracking of medium-weight hydrocarbons from
petroleum into smaller molecules to produce lighter forms like gasoline.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">There
are two kinds of pyrolysis technologies classified by heat source. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Direct-Heat Pyrolysis</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
method allows the heat source to make direct contact with the feedstock
material. It has the advantage of being the most efficient method of thermal
conductivity. Examples of Direct-Heat Pyrolysis systems are; steam pyrolysis
systems, nitrogen or argon gas pyrolysis systems. Both steam and gas pyrolysis
heat the feedstock material completely thereby decomposing the hydrocarbons.
The disadvantage of the Direct-Heat Pyrolysis method is that it requires the
consumption of a large amount of energy. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Indirect-Heat Pyrolysis</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the Indirect-Heat Pyrolysis method the feedstock material does not make direct
contact with the heat source. The material is loaded in a vacuum chamber
isolated from air. Then a heat source is applied to heat the chamber. The heat
source can be a burner or heat wire.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Indirect-Heat
Pyrolysis has a low thermal conductive efficiency because no contact is made
with the surface of the feedstock material. To improve efficiency, Catalyst
Pyrolysis has been developed. It uses a catalyst to bring the heat in contact with
the feedstock material. If more than one catalyst is used the greater the heat
contact is made with the surface of the feedstock material and the efficiency
is thereby increased. Another method is break down the feedstock material into
the small pieces or to grind the feedstock into powder where the feedstock
material will react instantly. This technology is called Fast Pyrolysis. No
matter how the contact surface of the feedstock material is increased, the heat
will always be applied from the surface to the interior of the feedstock
material. When heat makes contact with the surface of the feedstock material,
it will form a hard shell preventing the heat from penetrating to the interior
of the feedstock material resulting in incomplete de-composition of the organic
compounds. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
QI System combines the steam Direct-Heat Pyrolysis and Indirect-Heat Pyrolysis
technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Traditional
pyrolysis technology is a one stage process. It is designed and engineered to
handle only one kind of uniform organic material during the same process. Also,
the thermal conditions will vary based on what type of feedstock material is
used; otherwise the feedstock material cannot be decomposed properly. The
carbon residue will contain an organic composition. These by-products are not
marketable. As a result, most pyrolysis systems can only process one type of
feed stock material. Mixed or varied feedstock materials cannot be processed.
For application in the waste management field where there are a variety of
waste materials in an unpredictable composition, a one stage process cannot be
accommodated. The QI System can process mixed feedstock material based on its
two stage pyrolysis technology. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
first stage acts as a pyrolysis mode. It converts most of the organic composition
to fuel oil at the critical cracking stage. To obtain the greatest amount of
fuel oil is the most important function in this stage. The second stage
simulates gasification, deep pyrolysis, carbon activated, and fuel gas
synthesis system. The purpose of the second stage is to decompose the residue
of organic compounds remaining after completion of the pyrolysis mode and
convert it to fuel gas. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<a name="_bclFooter6"></a><DIV>





<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
</DIV><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size=2><DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always">&nbsp;</div><a name="page_7"></a><a name="_bclPageBorder7"></a><DIV STYLE="WIDTH: 100%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%; PADDING-LEFT: 0%">

<a name="_bclHeader7"></a><DIV>





<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Energy efficiency by Steam with indirect thermal pyrolysis
technologies:</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
mentioned above, traditional pyrolysis technology uses the application of
indirect heat to a thermal reaction chamber. Because the thermal conductive
surface is small, significantly more time and energy is required to decompose
the organic compounds resulting in low efficiency. Another problem is created
when heat is applied to the surface of the feedstock material. When heat
contacts the surface of the feedstock material, it forms a crust which
restricts penetration of the heat to the interior of the feedstock material,
resulting in an incomplete decomposition of the organic compounds. The carbon
residue will also contain remnants of the organic compounds and becomes a
secondary waste.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
QI System uses steam as the main heat source to directly heat the material.
Steam is used to penetrate the feedstock material into the interior in order to
decompose the organic compounds. To generate the steam heat source requires
more energy however the QI System uses an energy recovery technology to
generate the steam required by using the fuel gas generated from the pyrolysis
process which creates an indirect heating chamber by the use of the same waste
heat source. The reaction chamber is supported by steam and indirect heat at
the same time. This process increases the efficiency of energy use. When the
pyrolysis system commences to generate fuel gas, enough fuel gas is produced to
support the heat source for the system without the need for any external energy
source. This creates energy cost savings.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">System Safety</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">There
are two conditions necessary in a pyrolysis system. The first is a vacuum
condition. During this phase, the organic compounds will decompose to fuel oil
and fuel gas. This fuel gas is rich in hydrogen. It is dangerous if contact is
made with air and is the major reason why explosions can occur at most
pyrolysis plants. The second condition is a high pressure phase. The higher the
pressure, the higher the conversion rate, however, the high pressure creates
instability in the system and can be explosive.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
an Indirect Heat pyrolysis system, carbon dust is mixed with oil (called &#8220;tar&#8221;)
vapors. These tar vapors while passing through the pipe to the condenser, stick
to the pipe as tar. The tar may eventually plug the pipe and since tar contains
sulfur it can corrode the pipe creating leaks causing the explosive fuel gas to
leak. This is the most common reason for explosions in traditional pyrolysis
systems plants.&#160; To prevent such events, the QI System uses steam as
protection. The steam reacts with the carbon dust to generate more fuel gas and
reduces the tar produced. Also, the steam cleans the pipes to prevent corrosion
and forms a protective shell to protect the fuel gas from making contact with
the air even if it is leaking. The steam provides protection by preventing the
fuel from igniting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Markets</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">It
is our intention to market the QI System to sub-licensees and establish joint
ventures for waste conversion operations.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Effective
October 28, 2011, we entered into a Sub-License Agreement with Zhunger to grant
exclusive rights to sub-license, establish joint ventures to commercialize the
QI System, and use and process organic waste, and sell related by-products
generated from the QI System for a period of 25 years in the state of Johore,
Malaysia.&#160; Zhunger, as a sub licensee will be subject to a sub-license fee of $
70,000 payable in monthly installments of $ 5,000 per month commencing November
1, 2011 ending, January 1, 2013.&#160; As per our Agreement with Quadra, 5% of the
sub license fee is payable to Quadra on a quarterly basis.&#160; As additional
consideration, the joint venture will remit a 5% royalty fee on all gross sales
generated, of which 3% will be remitted to Quadra and 2% retained by us.&#160; We
have entered into discussions to establish waste conversion operations with
Zhunger through a joint venture however an agreement has not materialized.
There can be no assurance that any agreements will materialize. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Markets &#8211; By Products</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management is unaware of any plan for recycling of
used tires in Johore and Selangor, resulting in used tires being discarded as
garbage where they ultimately end up in landfills.&#160; We believe that these
discarded tires would provide a source of raw materials for us at little cost.&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font></p>


<a name="_bclFooter7"></a><DIV>





<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
</DIV><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size=2><DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always">&nbsp;</div><a name="page_8"></a><a name="_bclPageBorder8"></a><DIV STYLE="WIDTH: 100%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%; PADDING-LEFT: 0%">

<a name="_bclHeader8"></a><DIV>





<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sustainable biochar is a tool that can produce a soil
enhancer that holds carbon and makes soil more fertile; reduce agricultural
waste; and produce clean, renewable energy.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">Biochar is a highly porous charcoal that enables soil
to retain nutrients and water and carbon content and yields improved plant and
crop.&#160;&#160; The carbon content in the biochar can be stored in soil indefinitely.&#160;
Biochar as a soil enhancer is mostly used in areas that have depleted soils
with inadequate water and fertilizer use.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">Biochar can improve soil fertility for the long term
using locally available materials. Used alone, compost, manure or agrochemicals
must be added at the same rate every year in order to realize benefits.
Application rates can be reduced when nutrients are combined with biochar.
Biochar can play a role in expanding options for sustainable soil management,
not only to improve soil productivity but also to decrease nutrient loss
through leaching by percolating water.&#160; We intend to market biochar produced to
landscapers for softscape use in horticulture design.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Marketing Strategy </font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-GB style="font-size:10.0pt;">By-products generated would be initially marketed
throughout Malaysia.&#160; Our target market will be that of landscape
horticulturalists.&#160; We may expand our target market at a later time and such
efforts to expand our marketing scope will be dependent on the success of our
initial operations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Distribution Methods and Installation</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
currently do not have distribution methods to deliver by-products generated by
the System.&#160; We will explore methods of distribution subject to the market
response upon initiation of operations.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">New Products</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
are not developing nor do we intend to distribute any other products in the foreseeable
future.&#160;&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Competition</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management
is not aware of competition in Johore or Selangor.&#160;&#160; However emerging
competitors may have significantly greater financial, marketing and other
resources than we have.&#160; Competitors have and may adopt aggressive pricing or
inventory availability policies and devote substantially more resources to
website and systems development than we do. Increased competition may result in
reduced operating margins and loss of market share.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Availability of Raw Materials</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
are currently entering into discussions with several suppliers of used tires.&#160;
We have not entered into any definitive agreements with these suppliers.&#160; The
cost of the tires per ton will vary.&#160; Management is confident that these
sources are sufficient for supplying operations with the necessary feedstock
material.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
cannot estimate at this time the frequency of our placement of orders as we
have not established trends or possible seasonal aspects which may affect our
sub distributor&#8217;s business and the resultant increase or lag in number of
orders placed with us.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Orders and Payment</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payment
terms will vary and payments are made by wire transfer, bank draft, or money order.
</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Delivery</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Delivery
terms are subject to negotiations and are unique in each transaction. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<a name="_bclHeader9"></a><DIV>





<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Returns and Refunds</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our
warranty policy states that the QI System will be free from material defects in
materials and workmanship. The foregoing warranty is subject to the proper
installation, operation and maintenance of the QI System in accordance to the
QI System operating manual. Warranty claims must be made by the customer in
writing within 15 days of the manifestation of a problem. The warranty period
begins on the date the QI System is delivered and continues for Twelve (12)
months.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Excluded
from the warranty are problems due to accidents, misuse, misapplication,
storage damage, negligence, or modification to the QI System or its components.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Patents, Trademarks and Labor Contracts</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Patents</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We do not directly hold any patents for the QI System.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Trademarks</font></u></i><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;"> &nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
do not have any trademarks on our trade name or logo.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Labor Contracts</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
do not have any labor contracts. Once the QI System is fully operational, we
will require additional employees to operate the system and also sales staff
for marketing and sale of by-products generated.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p><p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Government Regulation</font></b></p><p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
are subject to regulations from various federal, state and municipal authorities,
each having different environment regulations to deal with waste and emissions.
The following are some of the regulatory authorities throughout the world.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the USA hazard wastes are regulated by the Environmental Protection Agency (&#8220;</font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">EPA</font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#8221;)
through the </font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Resource Conservation and Recovery Act</font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;"> (&#8220;</font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">RCRA</font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#8221;) which
requires that hazard wastes be tracked from the time that they are generated
until their final disposition. Further with the enactment of the </font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Comprehensive
Environmental Response, Compensation and Liability Act </font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">in 1980, a super
fund was created for the clean-up and remediation of closed and abandoned
hazardous waste sites. A facility that treats, stores or disposes of hazardous
waste must obtain a permit under the RCRA. Individual states may regulate
particular wastes more stringently than that mandated by the EPA because the
EPA is authorized to delegate primary rulemaking to individual States and most
states have implemented such regulations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
federal government also mandates the requirements for hazardous waste landfill
sites together with state and local governmental agencies which may have
criteria of their own and which in some cases may be more stringent than the federal
regulations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Worldwide
the United Nations Environmental Program (&#8220;</font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">UNEP</font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#8221;) estimated that more
than 400 million tons of hazardous waste is produced annually. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the United Kingdom the Department for Environment Food and Rural Affairs is the
agency responsible for policy and regulations on the environment which includes
air quality, waste operations and local authority environmental regulation. In Europe the European Commission is the regulator authority responsible issuing directives
for the regulation of hazardous waste.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
EPA is also the regulatory authority governing vehicle emissions and emissions
from large Municipal Waste Combustors (&#8220;</font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">MWC</font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#8221;) (greater than 250 tons per
day), small MSWs (less than 150 Tons per day) (MWCs are incinerators which burn
household, commercial/retail and or institutional waste), Hazardous Waste
Combusters (&#8216;</font><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">HWC</font></i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#8221;) and Medical Waste Incinerators. State or federal MWC
plans also include source and emission </font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">inventories,
emission limits, testing, monitoring and reporting requirements or site
specific compliance schedules including increments of progress.</font></p>
<a name="_bclFooter9"></a><DIV>





<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
</DIV><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size=2><DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always">&nbsp;</div><a name="page_10"></a><a name="_bclPageBorder10"></a><DIV STYLE="WIDTH: 100%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%; PADDING-LEFT: 0%">

<a name="_bclHeader10"></a><DIV>





<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>


<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Asian countries also have their own emission and waste treatment regulatory
bodies, most of which conform either to the EU or EPA standards.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
worldwide emissions levels have increased dramatically, a greater understanding
of the impacts of these emissions have resulted in increased regulation and new
development practices have been implemented to reduce emissions in countries
worldwide. All of the above are the regulatory environment in which our
technology and the proposed applications of the technology are applicable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Research and Development</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
intend to establish a research and development facility in each assembly plant
with the intention of maintaining the technological lead in terms of product
quality and development of new product applications. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-top:12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><b><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compliance with Environmental Laws</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">To
our knowledge, we are not subject to any environmental laws which are cause of
concern among management.&#160;&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;"><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;">Handling and Storage of Biochar</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; &nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the best of management&#8217;s knowledge, there are no guidelines or
precautions relating to the handling and storage of biochar.&#160; We intend on
handling and storing biochar based on standards applicable to carbon black as
we may expand our operations in the future to accommodate the production of
carbon black derived from waste tires. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">In general, pure carbon black is difficult to ignite, does not
undergo spontaneous combustion, and is not a dust explosion hazard. Red hot
metal and electric sparks will not cause carbon black dust to ignite
explosively. However, carbon black can be ignited by an open flame, glowing metal,
sparks or lighted cigarettes. Once ignited it burns slowly with the production
of toxic carbon monoxide. Storage fires may go undetected for some time, unless
stirred or if sparks are present. If impurities are present on the carbon black
(e.g. oil), then there is a risk of dust explosions. The risk of dust
explosions is increased by the presence of unconsumed oil that adheres to the
carbon.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Carbon black is a toxic solid. It may also be a dust explosion
hazard depending on the impurities present. It is necessary that engineering
controls are operating and that protective equipment requirement and personal
hygiene measures are being followed.&#160;&#160; Only authorized personnel should have
access to this material. They should be properly trained regarding its hazards
and its safe use.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">There should be no possible ignition sources, (e.g. sparks, open
flames). It is very important to keep areas where this material is used clear
of other materials which can burn (e.g. cardboard, sawdust). If impurities are
present on the carbon black this could be at risk of being an explosion
hazard.&#160; A non-sparking ventilation system, explosion-proof equipment and
intrinsically safe electrical systems in areas of use must be installed.&#160;&#160;
Carbon black should be stored in dust-tight, labeled containers and should be
kept closed when not in use.&#160;&#160; Methods to control hazardous conditions include
mechanical ventilation, local exhaust ventilation, and process enclosure if
necessary, to control airborne dust. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><u><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Handing and Storage of Fuel Oil </font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fuel oil has a high vapor pressure, evaporating quickly and will
go stale in a few weeks if not chemically treated. It has high ignition
temperature (about 1100&#176; F). Stored fuel oil must be treated with a
butylhydroxytoluene additive and protected from moisture if it is to be stored
for any length of time.&#160; Fuel tanks should be stored in a well-ventilated area
building. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<a name="_bclFooter10"></a><DIV>





<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=X-NONE style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
</DIV><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size=2><DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always">&nbsp;</div><a name="page_11"></a><a name="_bclPageBorder11"></a><DIV STYLE="WIDTH: 100%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%; PADDING-LEFT: 0%">

<a name="_bclHeader11"></a><DIV>





<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





</DIV>
<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Any electrical fixtures surrounding the
fuel oil tank should be explosion proof (sealed) and wired in sealed conduit to
prevent fuel vapors from coming into contact with electrical sparks. Smoking or
carrying of smoking materials within 50 feet of the fuel pumps should be
prohibited. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Employees</font></u></b><b><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;"> &nbsp;</font></u></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-top:12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc254620943"></a><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of to date, we had no full-time employees and no part-time employees.&#160; We
have engaged a consultant who provides various services to our company. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><i><u><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Principal Business Office &amp; Administrative Branch Office</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:0in;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:0in;text-align:justify;"><font color=black face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our administrative office for North American investor relations
and U.S. regulatory reporting is located at 10300 Charleston 10-56, Las Vegas,
NV, 89135. T</font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">elephone: 702-666-4298,
Facsimile: 702-543-3942.&#160; Our company President, Mr. Samuels provides office
space located at 26 Black Birch Way, # 15587, Kingston 6, Jamaica, WI and there
is no charge for use of this office space.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin-bottom:3.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:normal;">ITEM 1A. &#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; RISK
FACTORS</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">Any of the following
risks could materially adversely affect our business, financial condition, or operating
results.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">All
parties and individuals reviewing this Annual Report on Form 10K and considering
us as an investment should be aware of the financial risk involved. When deciding
whether to invest&#160; or&#160; not,&#160; careful&#160; review of the risk factors set forth herein
and&#160; consideration&#160; of&#160; forward-looking&#160; statements&#160; contained in this registration&#160;
statement&#160; should&#160; be&#160; adhered to. Prospective investors should be aware of the
difficulties encountered as we face all the risks including competition, and the
need for additional working capital. The likelihood of our success must be considered
in light of the problems and expenses that are frequently encountered in connection
with operations in the competitive environment in which we will be operating. </font></p>

<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">***You should read the following risk factors carefully
before purchasing our common stock. ***</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align=center style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">RISKS RELATING TO OUR BUSINESS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have a limited operating history upon which an evaluation of our prospects can be made.&#160; For that reason, it would be difficult for a potential investor to judge our prospects for success.</font></i></b></p><p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p><p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We were organized in March 2011. We entered into the Agreement with Quadra on February 8, 2012.&#160; We have had limited operations since our inception from which to evaluate our business and prospects.&#160; There can be no assurance that our future proposed operations will be implemented successfully or that we will have the ability to generate profits.&#160; If we are unable to sustain our operations, you may lose your entire investment.&#160; We face all the risks inherent in a new business, including the expenses, difficulties, complications and delays frequently encountered in connection with conducting operations, including capital requirements and management's potential underestimation of initial and ongoing costs.&#160; As a new business, we may encounter delays and other problems in connection with the methods of product distribution that we implement.&#160; We also face the risk that we will not be able to effectively implement our business plan.&#160; In evaluating our business and prospects, these difficulties should be considered.&#160; If we are not effective in addressing these risks, we will not operate profitably and we may not have adequate working capital to meet our obligations as they become due.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">If we do not receive shareholder loans we may be unable to continue
meeting our minimum funding requirements.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
will require shareholder loans to meet our working capital needs; however, we
have no formalized agreements with shareholders guaranteeing that any required
funding will be available to us.&#160; We may exhaust this source of funding at any
time, which would cause us to cease operations.&#160;&#160; </font></p>

To meet our needs for engineers and professional services personnel, we may use more costly third-party contractors and consultants to supplement our own staff. Our business may be harmed if we are unable to establish and maintain relationships with third-party implementation providers.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">We require short term funding in the amount of approximately $30,000 in the next 12 months to fund our operations.&nbsp; Although our shareholders are committed to providing the necessary funding in order to generate revenues they are not obligated to do so.&nbsp; We have no formal agreements with our shareholders.&nbsp; If we do not receive shareholder loans or any other form of funding, our operations would cease indefinitely.&nbsp; </FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><EM><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT></B></EM>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><EM><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT></B></EM>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><EM><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">We may not be able to compete effectively against our competitors, which could force us to curtail or cease business operations.</FONT></B></EM></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Many of our competitors have significantly greater name recognition, financial resources and larger distribution channels.&nbsp; If we are not able to compete effectively against our competitors, we will be forced to curtail or cease our business operations. We do not have any market share in the industry at this time.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><B><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="times new roman">We may face product liability for the product we sell.</FONT></I></B></P>

<H5 style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman"></FONT></I>&nbsp;</H5>

<H5 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-STYLE: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman">We may become liable for any damage caused by our products when used in the manner intended.&nbsp; Any such claim of liability, whether meritorious or not, could be time-consuming and result in costly litigation.&nbsp; We do not carry insurance.&nbsp; Any imposition of liability could severely harm our business.</FONT><B><FONT style="FONT-STYLE: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman"> &nbsp;</FONT></B></H5>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><B><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA face="times new roman">We are dependent on the services of our President and the loss of her services could have a material adverse effect on our ability to carry on business.</FONT></I></B></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA face="times new roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA face="times new roman">We are substantially dependent upon the efforts and skills of our company President, Mr. Locksley Samuels. We do not have an employment contract and thus she has no obligation to fulfill his capacities as President for any specified period of time.&nbsp;&nbsp; The loss of the services of Mr. Samuels will have a material effect on our business in that we would not have the necessary leadership to continue operations. </FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA face="times new roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><B><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA face="times new roman">Our shareholders may not be able to enforce U.S. civil liabilities claims.</FONT></I></B></P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Our assets are located outside the United States and all of our director and officers are located outside the United States.&nbsp; As a result, it may be difficult to effect service of process within the United States upon these persons.&nbsp; In addition, a shareholder should not assume that the courts in any other country (i) would enforce judgments of U.S. courts obtained in actions against us or such persons predicated upon the civil liability provisions of the U.S. federal securities laws or other laws of the United States, or (ii) would enforce, in original actions, liabilities against us or such persons predicated upon the U.S. federal securities laws or other laws of the United States.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><B><FONT style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt" align=center><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">RISKS RELATED TO OUR COMMON STOCK</FONT></B></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt" align=center><STRONG><FONT size=2></FONT></STRONG>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><B><I><FONT style="BACKGROUND: white; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA color=black face="Times New Roman">FINRA sales practice requirements may also limit a stockholder&#8217;s ability to buy and sell our stock.</FONT></I></B></P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-CA color=black face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="BACKGROUND: white; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA color=black face="Times New Roman">In addition to the penny stock rules promulgated by the SEC, FINRA rules require that in recommending an investment to a customer, a broker-dealer must have reasonable grounds for believing that the investment is </FONT>


<FONT style="BACKGROUND: white; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-CA color=black face="Times New Roman">suitable for that customer. Prior to recommending speculative low priced securities to their non-institutional customers, broker-dealers must make reasonable efforts to obtain information about the customer&#8217;s financial status, tax status, investment objectives and other information. Under interpretations of these rules, FINRA believes that there is a high probability that speculative low priced securities will not be suitable for at least some customers. FINRA requirements make it more difficult for broker dealers to recommend that their customers buy our common stock, which may limit the ability to buy and sell our stock and have an adverse effect on the market value for our shares.</FONT></P>

<a name="_bclFooter12"></a><DIV>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt" align=center><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt" align=center><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman">12</FONT></P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt" lang=X-NONE face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></DIV></DIV>
