<h2 style="margin-bottom:3.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:normal;">ITEM 11.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; EXECUTIVE COMPENSATION</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><b><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:0in;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">The particulars of the compensation
paid to the following persons:</font></p>

<p align=left style="margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face=symbol lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:7.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">our principal executive officer;</font></p>

<p align=left style="margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face=symbol lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:7.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">each of our two most highly compensated executive officers who
were serving as executive officers at the end of the years ended June 30, 2012
and 2011; and</font></p>

<p align=left style="margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face=symbol lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="times new roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:7.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">up to two additional individuals for whom disclosure would have
been provided under (b) but for the fact that the individual was not serving as
our executive officer at the end of the years ended June 30, 2012 and 2011,</font></p>

<p style="margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:0in;"><font face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">who we will collectively

following summary compensation table, except that no disclosure is provided for

conditions set forth in that certain common stock purchase agreement (the
&#8220;Common Stock Purchase Agreement&#8221;).&#160; We sold these shares of Common Stock under
the exemption from registration provided Regulation S.&#160; A form of the Common
Stock Purchase Agreement is attached hereto as Exhibits 10.1.</font></p>

6, Jamaica, WI and there is no charge for use of this office space.</font></p>

compensatory plans or arrangements with respect to our executive officers
resulting from their resignation,
retirement or other termination of employment or from a change of control. </font></p>

<P style="MARGIN: 12pt 0in 0pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Option Exercises </FONT></B></P>

<P style="MARGIN: 12pt 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">During our Fiscal year ended June 30, 2012 there were no options exercised by our named officers</FONT><B><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">. &nbsp;</FONT></I></B></P>

<P style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Compensation of Directors</FONT></B></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">We do not have any agreements for compensating our directors for their services in their capacity as directors, although such directors are expected in the future to receive stock options to purchase shares of our common stock as awarded by our board of directors. </FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">We have determined that none of our directors are independent directors, as that term is used in Item 7(d)(3)(iv)(B) of Schedule 14A under the </FONT><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Securities Exchange Act of 1934</FONT></I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">, as amended, and as defined by Rule 4200(a)(15) of the NASDAQ Marketplace Rules.</FONT></P>

<P style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN-LEFT: 0in; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0in"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Pension, Retirement or Similar Benefit Plans </FONT></B></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">There are no arrangements or plans in which we provide pension, retirement or similar benefits for directors or executive officers. We have no material bonus or profit sharing plans pursuant to which cash or non-cash compensation is or may be paid to our directors or executive officers, except that stock options may be granted at the discretion of the board of directors or a committee thereof.</FONT><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"> &nbsp;</FONT></B></P>

<P style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="Times New Roman">Indebtedness of Directors, Senior Officers, Executive Officers and Other Management </FONT></B></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="Times New Roman">None of our directors or executive officers or any associate or affiliate of our company during the last two fiscal years, is or has been indebted to our company by way of guarantee, support agreement, letter of credit or other similar agreement or understanding currently outstanding. </FONT></P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<H2 style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; TEXT-INDENT: -1in; MARGIN: 12pt 0in 3pt 1in"><A name="_Toc254620960"></A><B><FONT style="FONT-STYLE: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" face=Arial,sans-serif>ITEM 12.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; SECURITY OWNERSHIP OF CERTAIN BENEFICIAL OWNERS AND MANAGEMENT </FONT></B></H2>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">The following table sets forth information regarding the beneficial ownership of our shares of common stock as of June 30, 2012 (i) each person known by us to be the beneficial owner of more than 5% of our outstanding shares of common stock, (ii) each of our directors, (iii) each of our executive officers, and (iv) by all of our directors and executive officers as a group.&nbsp; Each person named in the table, has sole voting and investment power with respect to all shares shown as beneficially owned by such person and can be contacted at our executive office address.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">The persons or entities listed below have sole voting and investment power with respect to all shares of common stock beneficially owned by them, except to the extent such power may be shared with a spouse.&nbsp; No change in control is currently being contemplated.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt 27pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<DIV align=left>

<TABLE style="WIDTH: 495.899pt; BORDER-COLLAPSE: collapse" border=0 cellSpacing=0 cellPadding=0>



<TR style="PAGE-BREAK-INSIDE: avoid">

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Under Rule 13d-3 of the Exchange Act a beneficial owner of a security includes any person who, directly or indirectly, through any contract, arrangement, understanding, relationship, or otherwise has or shares: (i) voting power, which includes the power to vote, or to direct the voting of shares; and (ii) investment power, which includes the power to dispose or direct the disposition of shares. </FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>

<H2 style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 12pt 0in 3pt"><A name="_Toc254620961"></A><B><FONT style="FONT-STYLE: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" face=Arial,sans-serif>ITEM 13.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; CERTAIN RELATIONSHIPS AND RELATED TRANSACTIONS, AND DIRECTOR INDEPENDENCE</FONT></B></H2>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">On March 22, 2011, we issued an aggregate of 21,600,000 shares of Common Stock to Locksley Samuels for consideration of $2,160, pursuant to the terms and conditions set forth in that certain common stock purchase agreement (the &#8220;Common Stock Purchase Agreement&#8221;).&nbsp; We sold these shares of Common Stock under the exemption from registration provided Regulation S.&nbsp; A form of the Common Stock Purchase Agreement is attached hereto as Exhibits 10.1.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 0.5in; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Mr. Samuels provides office space located at 26 Black Birch Way, # 15587, Kingston 6, Jamaica, WI and there is no charge for use of this office space.</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Effective December 5, 2011, we entered into share subscription agreements with 32 shareholders for the sale of 11,401,000 common shares at $ 0.001 per share for total proceeds of $ 11,401.&nbsp; Each of the 32 shareholders holds less than 5% of the outstanding shares.&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT size=2></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="Times New Roman">The common stock issuance was exempt from registration pursuant to Regulation S promulgated under the Act. We have complied with the requirements of Regulation S by having no directed selling efforts made in the United States, ensuring that the investors are non-U.S. persons with addresses in a foreign country and having the investors make representation to us certifying that he or she is not a U.S. person and is not acquiring the common stock for the account or benefit of a U.S. person, other than persons who purchased common stock in transactions exempt from the registration requirements of the Securities Act; and also agrees only to sell the common stock in accordance with the registration provisions of the Act or an exemption there from, or in accordance with the provisions of the Regulation.</FONT></P>

<P style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman"></FONT></I>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">Director Independence</FONT></I></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0in 0in 6pt"><A name="_Toc254620962"></A><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">We currently act with one director, consisting of Locksley Samuels. We have determined that our director is not an &#8220;independent director&#8221; as defined in NASDAQ Marketplace Rule 4200(a)(15).</FONT></P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 12pt 0in 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="Times New Roman">We do not have a standing audit, compensation or nominating committee, but our entire board of directors acts in such capacities.&nbsp; We believe that our members of our board of directors are capable of analyzing and evaluating our financial statements and understanding internal controls and procedures for financial reporting. The board of directors of our company does not believe that it is necessary to have an audit committee because we believe that the functions of an audit committee can be adequately performed by the board of directors. In addition, we believe that retaining an independent director who would qualify as an &#8220;audit committee financial expert&#8221; would be overly costly and burdensome and is not warranted in our circumstances given the early stages of our development.</FONT></P>

<H2 style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; MARGIN: 12pt 0in 3pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-STYLE: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" face=Arial,sans-serif>ITEM 14.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; PRINCIPAL ACCOUNTANT FEES AND SERVICES</FONT></B></H2>
